āvase varṣāṣāṭi nikṣipet* /

vā jalāntaritatvaṃ gantavyasyety asyābhāvenādattasamvṛttir aṇāstīrṇakaṭhinaḥ saṃghāṭīṃ*

Vin_2.599 / mūlāmūlādeś ca /

**(Vin_2,4,6) kuladūṣaṇam /
Vin_2.971 / saṃmanyeran pāpayor bhikṣubhikṣuṇyoḥ kulapratisaṃvedakam /
Vin_2.972 / śṛṇvantvāyuṣmanto kuleṣu kuladūṣakā āśrameṣv āśramadūṣakās tadyathā sampanne
śālikṣetre 'śanirvicakrā nipated yāvad eva tasyaiva śāler utsādāya vināśāyānayena
vyasanāya saṃpanne vā ikṣukṣetre mañjiṣṭhi[19a1]kā nāma rogajātir niyate[d] yāvad
eva tasyaivekṣor utsādāya vināśāyānayena vyasanāya mā yūyam āyuṣmanto 'nena bhikṣunānayā
bhikṣuṇyā śāsanaṃ pramiṇuta eṣa bhikṣur eṣā ca bhikṣuṇī dagdhena dhānā aprarohaṇadharmā
asmin dharmavinaye bhagavantaṃ paśyata sthavirasthavirāṃś ca bhikṣūn śniti kuleṣu
kulapratisaṃvedako brūyāt /
Vin_2.973 / anutsahamāne [19a2] jñaptiṃ kuryuḥ /
// [iti] kuladūṣaṇam // 6 //

*Vin_3. vārṣikavastu /
**(Vin_3,1) tadgrāhakasammatiḥ /
Vin_3.1 varṣā upagacchet* /

āpādakaṭhillakāta /

**(Vin_3,2) śalākāñ cāraṇam /
Vin_3.10 / apāraṇe nekasya /
Vin_3.11 / so ktagandhaiś cāṅgerīpaṭalakagate śukle vāsasy upanikṣiptāḥ śalākā vṛddhānte
niveśyā yañ cāyaṃ cāsminn āvāse kriyākāro yo yusmākam utsahate tena kriyākāreṇāsminn
āvāse varṣāvastuṃ sa śalākāṃ grihṇātu na ca vaḥ kenacid antarvarṣe saṃghamadhye raṇam
utpā[42a2]dayitavyo yo vaḥ kasyacit kiñcij jānāti sa idānīṃ* vadanta yo ntarvarṣe
saṃghe raṇam utpādayiṣyati tasya saṃgha uttara upaparīkṣitavyaṃ matsyata iti bhikṣūn vedayeta /
Vin_3.12 / grahaṇopaśamanaṃ prati saṃghaṃ jñapayed anyaḥ /

*Vin_4. pravāraṇavastu /

sarvarātrikadharmaśravaṇadāpanam* /

/ svakyena vastunā vastapravāraṇam ārabheta vacanato gṛhītvā ḥ [43b6] saṃghena labhyaṃ bhadantā evaṃ rūpeṇāpi vastunā varṣoṣitam

pravārayed antarvarṣa prakramiṣyan* karaṇīyena /

**(Vin_4,2) kṣudrakādigatam /

Vin_4.56 / na vilaṃghayet* /

*Vin_5. kaṭhinavastu /

Vin_5.1 / āstrīṇvīran* kaṭhinam* /
Vin_5.2 / yathā trayam evam āstīrṇasya paraṃparabhojanam api nirdoṣaṃ gaṇabhojanaman āmantryagrāmapraveśaś cīvaravijñapanañ ca /

*Vin_10, pratikriyāvastu /
**(Vin_10,1) pratikriyāvastu /
Vin_10.1 / nāpratikṛtājñapanajaṣkarma pratyanubhavet /
Vin_10.2 / utsṛjya poṣadhaṃ pravāraṇāñ ca /
Vin_10.3 / na sīmāntarasthasya kasmiṃś cid aṅgatvam /
Vin_10.4 / dhvaṃsas tadgatau sāhya gatasya /
Vin_10.5 / ubhayasthatvam ekasminn e[55a4]katra pāde parasmin paratra /
Vin_10.6 / sarvasminn avaṣṭambhini sthitasyāvaṣṭabdhe /
Vin_10.7 / rūḍhir evam anekatropagateḥ /
Vin_10.8 / arhatvam anekaśayanāsanagrāhe /
Vin_10.9 / yatheṣṭam asya vastavyatā /
Vin_10.10 / na vyagrakāritvaṃ jinasya /
Vin_10.11 / na pūrakatvam /
Vin_10.12 / nākarmaṇā tatkaraṇīyasyotthānam /
Vin_10.13 / kṛtatvaṃ yadbhūyas kṛtatve vākyasyānuttarasya /
Vin_10.14 / nākīrttitve nimittānāṃ bandhe /
Vin_10.15 / pārivāsike [55a5] nāntasyopasthānasaṃvṛteḥ /
Vin_10.16 / unmattakena coddeśasya /
Vin_10.17 / jñaptivad bhedānuṣṭhānam /
Vin_10.18 / anaṅgam atra bhinnavyaṃjanatvam /
Vin_10.19 / na hāsyabhāvena kasyacit sthūlam arūḍhibuddhyā bhedotkṣepayoḥ /
Vin_10.20 / duṣkṛtam asaṃghabhūtatve /
Vin_10.21 / nānyeṣāṃ nānāsaṃvāsikebhyo barhāṇāṃ pūraṇe gaṇena jñaptivācanayoḥ /
Vin_10.22 / nāsaṃpannatve 'rha[ḥ] svasaṃghena pratyanubhavasya /

kramavyatyād arūḍhiḥ /

samīcīm upadarśayato viramato nimittād avasāraṇaṃ yācite /

Vin_10.137 / nāsanaṃ paribhuñjīta /
Vin_10.138 / na prajñaptān deyadharmaṃ /
Vin_10.139 / na piṇḍapātaṃ pratigṛhṇītāt /
Vin_10.140 / na dharmaṃ deśayet /
Vin_10.141 / yat karma karaṇaṃ tadgatānāṃ nikubjitatvam /
Vin_10.142 / anuttānam asyāsvapakṣakulaṃ pratyotkṣiptakāt /
Vin_10.143 / tetanamasya kenacit /
Vin_10.144 / kṣamitataty unmajjanaṃ jñapanena /
Vin_10.145 / bhavaty utthānam anutpannapraticchādacittasyāntimātaḥ /
Vin_10.146 / śikṣācaraṇena /
Vin_10.147 / [56b3] tallabhāyāḥ saṃghataḥ /
Vin_10.148 / karmaṇā dānam /
Vin_10.149 / yāvaj jīva[m] /
Vin_10.150 / śuddhir ekasya purato deśanena saṃghāvaśeṣato hrīmataḥ /
Vin_10.151 / sūtradharasya vinayasya mātṛkāyāḥ /
Vin_10.152 / jñātasya ca /
Vin_10.153 / aśayatāpattivyutthānena daṇḍakarmataḥ /
Vin_10.154 / nikāyato nāmātrāpatter nāma /
Vin_10.155 / samutthānaṃ gotram /
// samāptaṃ pratikriyāvastu // 10 //
*Vin_11, kālākālasampātavastu /
**(Vin_11,1) kālākālasampātavstu /
Vin_11.1 / apratītatve saṃghāvaśeṣāntardhāne [56b4] ntāsthitapratichādacittasyāśaktavattāyāṃ
kṛtaṃ ne vā kiṃ* vā kīdṛśyaṃ ceti smartum anupasaṃpa katotkṣiptayoś cānutthānaṃ pratichādasya /
Vin_11.2 / bhraṣṭasyāvahārikasaṃjñatāyām āpatter asyāparājayāt* /
Vin_11.3 / aprajñaptatāyāṃ ca /
Vin_11.4 / nājñātatvena sraddhitatve vā /
Vin_11.5 / anabhijñatāsaṃjñino pi /
Vin_11.6 / bhūmyantarasthitāyāṃ prāco pi /
Vin_11.7 / jñānavat pratichāde vimatiḥ saṃghā[56b5]vaśeṣatvaṃ /
Vin_11.8 / āvaraṇasyāpi sābhūti yā pratichādānutthānasya /
Vin_11.9 / duṣkṛtam anādṛtyaiḥ caraṇotsarge /
Vin_11.10 / tanaikāyikādhyācāre cātra /
Vin_11.11 / saṃbhave cāpratikṛtau /
Vin_11.12 / tadavasthatvaṃ pratyāgatāvacaraṇabhūmeḥ /
Vin_11.13 / śodhite vastuni sāṣānuṣṭhānam anirjñāne pratichādakālasyāsaṃvya ānany ūnatvasya saṃśrayaṇaṃ /
Vin_11.14 / caritavyatāyāṃ śuddhāntikatvottarasya /
Vin_11.15 / catu[56b6]ro māsāṃ śuddhāntikam iti /
Vin_11.16 / aparimātvasyāpratichāde /
Vin_11.17 / saṃcintya śukre visṛṣṭa-samutthāma-parimāṇām iti /
Vin_11.18 / yāvatīṣv abhiprāyas tāvat kīmitvam atrātrānuṣṭhiteḥ /
Vin_11.19 / aparimāna ity anirjñāne sya saṃśrayasaṃbahulāḥ parimānavatya iti prābhūtye /
Vin_11.20 / atiriktena kālānāṃ /
Vin_11.21 / prabhṛtimatvena nāmnāṃ /
bhyām āditvena /
Vin_11.23 / carato paraprāksampannapraticikīrṣotpattau pṛ[tha]g* dānam ekaṃ caraṇaṃ /
Vin_11.24 / nāsya pratichannatāyāṃ mānāsye saṃbhavaḥ /
// [iti] kālākālasaṃpātavastu // 1 //
**(Vin_11,2) pṛcchāgatam /
Vin_11.25 / nānantye nse horātrasya pratichādotthānam* /
Vin_11.26 / nābhāve ṅgasyodbhāvanāyātmacittānā[ṃ] pratichādaḥ /
Vin_11.27 / abhāvamamatyapakrāntivaśasya /
Vin_11.28 / tadarthavaśatayāpi kṛtau /
Vin_11.29 / vinārthe[57a2]na duṣkṛtam /
Vin_11.30 / prātkānhyāt /
Vin_11.31 / anutsṛṣṭatvaṃ pratichādacittasya tatcittatānadorṣamāpatteḥ parājitasyāprakṛtau /

*Vin_12, bhūmyantarasthacaraṇavastu /
**(Vin_12,1) bhūmyantarasthacaraṇavastu /
Vin_12.1 / pārivāsikamānāsyacāribhyām abhivādanavandana-pratyutthānāṃjalisāmīcīkarmaṇāṃ prakṛtisthād bhikṣor asvīkaraṇaṃ /
Vin_12.2 / yasyābhyāmakaraṇam itarair api tatra tadgatasya /
Vin_12.3 / yad aparihāṇikāto nyathānena sārddham acaṃkra[57a3]maṇam /
Vin_12.4 / nīcatarāsanakatvād aniṣādaḥ /
Vin_12.5 / paścācchramaṇātmakatātaṣkulānupasaṃkramaṇaṃ /
Vin_12.6 / akalpanamekachadane śayyāyāḥ /
Vin_12.7 / pravrājanopasaṃpādananiḥśrayadānaśramaṇoddeśopasthāpanānām akaraṇaṃ /
Vin_12.8 / prajñaptivācanayoś cāpratīṣṭaḥ /
Vin_12.9 / karmakārakabhikṣuṇyavavādakasaṃghavaiśvāsikasammateḥ /
Vin_12.10 / avyāparaṇa prāksammatenāpi /
Vin_12.11 / anavava[57a4]danañ ca bhikṣuṇīnām* /
Vin_12.12 / anuddeśaḥ poṣadhe prātimokṣasya saty anyatroddeṣṭari /
Vin_12.13 / acodanaṃ vipattyā bhikṣoḥ /
Vin_12.14 / anapasāritasya saṃghāt* /
Vin_12.15 / akaraṇaṃ savacanīyatāsakīlatvayoḥ /
Vin_12.16 / asthāpanam avavādapoṣadhapravāraṇājñaptivācanānāṃ /
Vin_12.17 / asaṃprayogo nena /
Vin_12.18 / varjanaṃ kṛtadaṇḍanimittasya /
Vin_12.19 / anyasya cāparādhasya /
Vin_12.20 / nāparādhyatā sabrahmacāriṣu /
Vin_12.21 / [57a5] vratasya niḥsāraḥ pravartito bhavatīti manasikaraṇaṃ /
Vin_12.22 / kālyam utthāya dvāramokṣo dīpasthālakoddharaṇavihārasekasaṃmārgasukumārigomayakārṣyānupradānāni /
Vin_12.23 / dhāvanaṃ prasrāvoccārakuṭyāḥ /
Vin_12.24 / poccana-mṛtakālānurūpapānīyopasthāpanam* /
Vin_12.25 / praṇāḍikāmukhānāṃ dhāvanam* /
Vin_12.26 / āsanaṃ prajñapanam* /
Vin_12.27 / kālaṃ jñātvā dhūpatatkaṭacchukayor upasthapanama /
Vin_12.28 / [57a6] pratibalatā vecchāsturguṇāsaṃkīrtaṇaṃ /
Vin_12.29 / na ced bhāṣaṇakādhyeṣaṇaṃ /
Vin_12.30 / upanvāhṛte gaṇḍīdānam* /
Vin_12.31 / dharmaś ced bhikṣūṇāṃ vījanam* /
Vin_12.32 / antyatvam asya sarvopasaṃpannānām /
Vin_12.33 / kṛte bhaktakṛtye śayanāsanasya channe gopanam* /
Vin_12.34 / pātrādhiṣṭhānachoraṇaṃ* /
Vin_12.35 / kālaṃ jñātvā stūpānāṃ saṃmārjanam* /
Vin_12.36 / sukumārigomayakārṣyanupradānaṃ /
Vin_12.37 / sāmagrīvelāyāṃ pra[57b1]jñapanādyāguṇagatāt* /
Vin_12.38 / pratibalatā ced divasārocanam* /
Vin_12.39 / na ced anyasya bhikṣor adhyeṣaṇaṃ /
Vin_12.40 / pādaśocanaṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ caikālikaṃ kālānurūpeṇāmbunā /
Vin_12.41 / mrakṣaṇañ cānicchāyāṃ snehopasaṃhāraḥ /
Vin_12.42 / vihāre 'sya pratyante rhatvaṃ /
Vin_12.43 / arhatvaṃ sarvatra lābhe /
Vin_12.44 / pratijāgriyāt kuśalapakṣe /
Vin_12.45 / tadvad atra tatprabhāvaiṣīyaśikṣādattakau /

/ arūḍair aprakṛtistheṣu paripāsamānāpy aśikṣācaraṇānāṃ / [end of R om.]
Vin_12.46 / asaṃghe ca /
Vin_12.47 / [57b3] paricchinneṣu ca tadāśramapadopagebhyaḥ /
Vin_12.48 / na bahutāṃ pariharet* /
Vin_12.49 / sa sthaviraprātimokṣatāyai prayateta /
Vin_12.50 / na yatryānye triḥprabhṛtayaḥ sarvathā tadākhyacaraṇās tatra taccaret* /
Vin_12.51 / nānyatra prathamāvaraṇeṇānudgamayenāṃ /
Vin_12.52 / varttsyat vṛttam ārocayetāṃ /
Vin_12.53 / saṃnipāte saṃghasya /
Vin_12.54 / pratyahaṃ na cec ciraṃ caritavyatvaṃ /
Vin_12.55 / atra tricaturaiḥ /
Vin_12.56 / naivānenārthenāvaspaṇḍayet* /
Vin_12.57 / [57b4] kalahakārakāgamanañ ca śrutvā bhayañ cedataḥ pratini[ḥ]sṛjetāṃ saṃghasannidhau pudgale vā /
Vin_12.58 / apagatau bhīter ādānaṃ tatraivaṃ /

**(Vin_12,2) pṛcchāgatam /
Vin_12.59 / chedas tadahorātrasya prakṛtisthena sārdham ekachadane parivāsikamānāsyacāriṇoḥ śayyāyāṃ bahi[ḥ]sīmni ca /
Vin_12.60 / anārocane ca /

Vin_12.62 / na parivāsikena sārdham ekachadane pārivāsikaḥ śayīt* /

*Vin_13. parikarmavastu
Vin_13.1 // nāprāsiddhikasya mūlatvaṃ /
Vin_13.2 / arūḍhir avasitapravāraṇoktau pravāraṇāsthāpanasya /
Vin_13.3 / tathā glānakartṛkatāyāṃ /
Vin_13.4 / dūtenāpi /
Vin_13.5 / glānagatāyāñ ca /
Vin_13.6 / [57b6] naitat pratīccheyuḥ /
Vin_13.7 / āgamaya tvam āyuṣmaṃ glānas tvam aprayojyama ity āyusmaṃ bhūteti glāno sāv ananuyojyā iti prativadeyuḥ /
Vin_13.8 / anavagatasvarūpatāyāṃ kṛtasya kartur vā codanasya /
Vin_13.9 / śiṣṭe pi nākāle pravarteta /
Vin_13.10 / nānupasthāsya smṛtisaṃprajanye /
Vin_13.11 / nānekānte /
Vin_13.12 / nākāritāvakāśe /
Vin_13.13 / tatvaṃ pravāraṇasya /
Vin_13.14 / asmṛtau smāraṇaṃ [58a1] /
Vin_13.15 // akaraṇebhyaḥ vacanīyatām asya kuryāt* /
Vin_13.16 / savacanīyaṃ tv āyuṣman karomi na tvaṃ yo smādāvāsādanavalokya prakramitavyam asti me āyuṣmati praṇihitaṃ vacanāyeti /
Vin_13.17 / āgacchaty eva damanāthamana codyatāṃ /
Vin_13.18 / ālapanāder asy anuvinivartanam* /
Vin_13.19 / tathāpi poṣadhasthāpanaṃ /
Vin_13.20 / tato pi pravāraṇāyāḥ /
Vin_13.21 / karaṇam asyatra sthāpakaiḥ sthāpitasya tena [58a2] sārdham upasāraṇaṃ /
Vin_13.22 / kṛtatve vakāśasyāmṛdutvaṃ cet sakīlakaraṇaṃ /
Vin_13.23 / vakṣyāmy atrāmutra vā vase mutra vā vāstuni yatra ceṣṭam ity āropya cāmattiṃ* darśayitvāparādham utsṛjanena /
Vin_13.24 / śīladṛṣṭyā cārājīva vipatyā sarvasyāsya codanādeḥ kriyāyāṃ ruḍhiḥ samūlakaṃ /
Vin_13.25 / na durdūlena kuryāt* /
Vin_13.26 / akaraṇam atra vastunaḥ satyatvaṃ /
Vin_13.27 / kriyānimittānāṃ parasaṃlāpa[58a3]sya sānuśrāvaṇasyeti trividhaṃ śrutaṃ /
Vin_13.28 / amūlatvam asraddhitasya /
Vin_13.29 / kāmo nekatve jñātuś codanādau /
Vin_13.30 / nāpravāraṇe tatsthāvanam* /
Vin_13.31 / nāpoṣadhe tasya na kṛtau kṛtatve vā strītve sthāpakasyai[ka]tarasya puṃstve sthāpitatvaṃ sthāpitatā /
Vin_13.32 / na naṣṭaprakṛtinā /
Vin_13.33 / nāśīlaikyena /
Vin_13.34 / nānayoḥ /
/ pārikarmaṇavastupṛcchā // 13
*Vin_14. karmabhedavastu
**(Vin_14,1) karmabhedaḥ
Vin_14.1 // na nānātvāya saṃghasya prabhāviṣṇum akā[58a4]maṃ codayed unmoṭayed vā codayatvaṃ /
Vin_14.2 / na yatra prativirodhas tena sārdham abhinamane samāsīta /
Vin_14.3 / dvitrāsanāntaritam anyatra /
Vin_14.4 / evam itaras tena /
Vin_14.5 / antaritasyānayor vihārasya deyatvaṃ grāhyatā ca /
Vin_14.6 / dharme vinaye caitadvatām adharme ced abhiniveśo jñātvā saṃghasāmagrīn na vidyate /
Vin_14.7 / tasmān na tad anyānāṃ saṃbhūya kṛtau karmaṇo rūḍhin na paraspareṇāvyagratvam* /
Vin_14.8 / [58a5] kaliparāyaṇatva eṣā tadvipakṣasya cāvandyatvam idaṃ dharmabhiḥ /
Vin_14.9 / pratyutthānāsanopanimantraṇāsaṃlapanālapanasaṃmodanavyavalokanālokanānām apy akaraṇaṃ /
Vin_14.10 / lūhaśayanāsanānupradānaṃ hastasaṃvyavahārakena /
Vin_14.11 / vacanenānyatra sasūtam ity aparam* /
Vin_14.12 / pratyante vihārasya /
Vin_14.13 / mṛddhadvā vayam iti vadatsu yūtham api śramaṇāḥ śākyaputriyā sma ity ātmānam* [58a6] pratijānīdhve /
Vin_14.14 / yeṣāṃ cedaṃ vṛttam iyaṃ vārtā kāruṇiko vaḥ śāstā yenaitad anujñātam etad api vo na prāpadyata iti prativadeyur anyatra /
Vin_14.15 / na bhikṣuṇyāsanamokṣaṃ hāpayet* /
Vin_14.16 / dadītopāsakapiṇḍapātam /
Vin_14.17 / nāpi sāritāām eṣāṃ sāmagyasya vinā sāmagrīlābhenotthāpanaṃ /
Vin_14.18 / na vinā poṣadhena prakṛtisthatāprāptiḥ /
Vin_14.19 / datvapinaṃ kuryuḥ /
Vin_14.20 / karmaṇaitat* /
Vin_14.21 / pūrvaṃ ca /
Vin_14.22 / [58b1] kalpate sāmagrīmaṅgalārthamāpadi poṣadhaḥ /
Vin_14.23 / tasyaiva cātra kālasya nimittatvaṃ /
/ karmabhedavastu //
**(Vin_14,2) pṛcchāgataḥ /
Vin_14.24 / karmaṇaḥ kṛtāvadharmavādibhir antaḥsīmni pṛthak tadbhedo tadacittena /
Vin_14.25 / rūḍhir asmin* pratisvaṃ karmaṇaḥ /
Vin_14.26 / nāsvapakṣaṃ prati /
Vin_14.27 / dharmavādi kṛtatā saṃghasya kṛtatvaṃ /
Vin_14.28 / sthalasthair atra sanni ced bhikṣuṇīnām acodyatvaṃ /
Vin_14.29 / vyagratvam eṣāṃ dharmapakṣaiḥ /
Vin_14.30 / dhvanso nuvidhau ta[58b2]ttvasya /
Vin_14.31 / nainaṃ kuryāt* /
Vin_14.32 / acodyatvam* pakṣāparapakṣavyavasthitasya bhikṣuṇīsaṃghasya /
Vin_14.33 / nainaḥ bhinnasya /
Vin_14.34 / samagrya yācamānānāṃ niyojyatvaṃ /
Vin_14.35 / dharmatrādini gāmitvaṃ vārṣikasya /
Vin_14.36 / ubhayasannipāte cāvibhajyāpratipātitasya saṃghe vaibhājyasya /
Vin_14.37 / saṃghaparimāṇatā cet tatra teṣāṃ /
Vin_14.38 / janatā cetir eṣām /
Vin_14.39 / tat tatā yadīyasyotsaṃghe pratipādanaṃ [58b3] dvayoś ced ubhayatra /
Vin_14.40 / pudgalaso rāṃśitvaṃ na saṃghaśaḥ /
/ karmabhedavastugate pṛcchā māṇavike // 14
*Vin_15. cakrabhedavastu /
Vin_15.1 / jñapanato vā pṛthagbhāvasya dharmāt saṃghabhedaḥ /
Vin_15.2 / śalākāgrahaṇato vānenārthena /
 Vin_15.3 / arūḍhir asyāsaṃghaparimāṇatve bhidyamānānām asatve cānyeṣām antaḥsīmni saṃghaparisānānām adharmadharmayoḥ tathātvena pratyavagatāv  #
ānantaryaṃ / 
Vin_15.4 / dharmasaṃjñi[58b4]no pi bhede /
/ cakrabhedavastu / 15
*Vin_16. adhikaraṇavastu
**(Vin_16,1) adhikaraṇam /
Vin_16.1 / catvāri saṃkṣopakaraṇāni /
Vin_16.2 / padārthatathātve vipratipattir varjanaṃ sāpattikā sāmagryadānaṃ karmāṇi /
Vin_16.3 / prathamanimittasyaikotīkaraṇena vyupaśamanam* /
Vin_16.4 / anena ca śuddhidāne ca dvitīyanimittasya /
Vin_16.5 / tritīyanimittasya pratikaraṇe nivāraṇaniyuktatvādānena ca /
Vin_16.6 / dāpanenāntyasya /
Vin_16.7 / sabhyai svayam aśaktau vivaditroḥ saṃpra[58b5]tipādanam* /
Vin_16.8 / bhikṣubhir abhirucitaiḥ /
Vin_16.9 / tayor ekataḥ sthalasthānārocanaṃ /
Vin_16.10 / sammatir eṣāṃ saṃghena sātatikānāṃ /
Vin_16.11 / anutdyojinaṣkalahe tra saṃmantavyatā /
Vin_16.12 / lajjinaḥ śikṣākāmasya /
Vin_16.13 / suviniścitasya vinaye /
Vin_16.14 / kuśalasyādhikaraṇavṛtte dhyācāre ca /
Vin_16.15 / viniviṣṭasya /
Vin_16.16 / dhīr asyāsaṃrabdhaya prasthānasya /
Vin_16.17 / samasya /
Vin_16.18 / avagantuḥ /
Vin_16.19 / pratyāyakasya /
Vin_16.20 / [58b6] viduṣaḥ /
Vin_16.21 / anupaśamane taiḥ /
Vin_16.22 / saṃghe nikṣepaḥ /
Vin_16.23 / asaktau tena vyūḍhānāṃ saṃmatiḥ /
Vin_16.24 / anūnānāṃ saṃghaparimāṇāt* /
Vin_16.25 / samantṛtvaṃ vargasya svato saktau vyūḍhakeṣu /
Vin_16.26 / akritāv uttarasyāsaktau yata ādānatantranikṣepaḥ /
Vin_16.27 / pratyāgate mūlasaṃghe nādhikaraṇasaṃcārakasaṃmatiḥ /
Vin_16.28 / tena sasthavire saprātimokṣe nyatra saṃgha upanikṣepaḥ /
Vin_16.29 / [59a1] // trimāsyāt kālasya dānaṃ vṛttārocanapūrvakaṃ /
Vin_16.30 / asyaitat* /
Vin_16.31 / pratyarpite tena sūtradharavinayadharamātṛkadhareṣu /
Vin_16.32 / ṣaṇmāsyāḥ /
Vin_16.33 / taiḥ prabhāvite sthavire aparyantasya /
Vin_16.34 / varjayed asau tataḥ svīkaraṇaṃ kasyacit* /

nāsti dvayor yudhyato jaya ekasya jaya ekasya parājayaḥ /

// śayanāsanavastu kṣudrakādigatam* //
// samāptañ ca śayanāsanavastu paścimaṃ // 17 //
Vinayakarmasaṃgrahakārikāḥ
dhāraṇaṃ vipravāsaṃ ca sparśam agner nivārite /
bhojanaṃ bījāghātaṃ ca deśe ca harite śuciḥ //
utsargaṃ vṛkṣārohaś ca śaikṣā u[65a5]ddeśāyos saha /
ratnasparśanabhukyā ca jātas sāṃnidhyānāntayoḥ //
bhūmiprarohaghātābhyām utsṛjyānta ca sūtragataṃ /
pravṛṣe katra vasanaṃ poṣadhas sapravāraṇāḥ //
ityādy asyāntabhāg liṅga yāñcā bhāṇḍopabhugdrava kāmopabhoga saṃvāsānād
arāśodhakavastukam /
sparśapañjaranikṣepau pratichādo nivāraṇam /
trayaṃ kiṃcitkacatuṣṭayaṃ [65a6] gaṇamṛtasīmni ratnataḥ //
chandasaṃmṛṣṭasaṃsparśāc catuṣṭayaṃ bhavati paścimam /
vidhāraṇaṃ saptakaṃ dve cānye dhāraṇādhiṣṭhānoddhārānuddhāra iti //
hiraṇyānyacīvarāsanavarṣakajanasaṃghārthaṃ vacanapalasaṃcataḥ niṣprayojane
hitvānuddhṛto cānuśāṭī ca dvādaśaparṣya nalaṣaṭkaṃ cīvaraṃ
saṃkṣepasyānvananuvyabhiśokabhaṇḍanam /
anvayāśikṣaṇānusthānāt /
[65b1] jatvaṅgulitalaromachannau ca karṇakagrahaṇe bhikṣoś ca vidyāpāṭhanamocana
saṃtagradhāraṇaṃ /
gṛhe channe layane mañce udvarttanamaṃcaka unmuroṭikā gandhapiṇyākataḥ /
snāośīraphalakurvatriśīrṣāṇāṃ kārṇaṅ kāravṛddhādi /
chatropānaha āsandī niṣādārikarttanaṃ coḍā //
vikrayagṛhapaticyutvā lasuna
rajādaka dhāvana dānaparivarttanataḥ [65b2] /
carṇakulāniṣkāsanantarur dṛṣṭa
sapatha vyathanāvasyaṇḍanakrośānasekāvyupaśayanataḥ /
chandāvavādapoṣadhavarṣaprāvaraṇakaṭhinoddhārabhājanavarṣākā[la?]caryācara-
ṇavādaḥ /
pṛcchā vahiśchoraṇe tiraḥ /
// bhikṣuṇīvibhaṅgoddhānam //
jñapanaṃ sekavākyañ ca satyavākyañ ca tadyathā /
rahontaḥ prasrayor arthapoṣadhasyātra sā yadi //
saṃghe [65b3] vaimatike cāsyāṃ vivādaniṣṭhitatvayoḥ
pravāraṇagate cātra sarvasminn ardhapañcake //
varṣopagamane caiva mṛtārthe prativastunā /
dāne kaṭhinavastrasya duṣṭhulārocane pi ca //
dāne vstrasya gaṇān catuṣke kulasamvṛti /
tatprasrabdhyau kubje ca sonmajje jñaptimātrakaṃ //
mukhasīmadvayāvipravāsonmattapravāraka /
śayyāsanagṛhagāṇāṃ [65b4] kalpabhūmeś ca sanmati //
kaṭhinasya tadāstartturuddhāro syāvasāraṇaṃ /
vihāro deśikādīnāṃ sthalasthavyūḍhanāyakaṃ //
śalākam vārakānāṃ vihārakuṭideśane /
codakasyāpravāsāya sanmetaṣyā tra cāriṇāḥ //
aprasādapravedāvavaditrorvanavedinaḥ /
avandanānalārthaṃ ca daṇḍaśikṣārtham eva ca //
ekalābhakriyāyāñ ca śikṣaṇā na samu[65b5]pasthite /
putre jñātau bahiryāne jñapanaṃ śaikṣyāvāsanaṃ //
upasaṃpādanaṃ tīrthyavāsadānaṃ [ca] mocanaṃ /
sīmnaḥ sāmragra dānaṃ ca poṣadhasya ca saptakaṃ //
ṣaṭkaṃ ca smṛtyasaṃmūḍha tatsvabhāvagamaṣṭakaṃ /
ājñaptadhvastadānaṃ ca jñapanaṃ satrivācanaṃ //
// vinayakarmasaṃgrahakārikāḥ samāptāḥ //
// samāptaṃ vinayasūtram /
[65b6] kṛtir ācāryaguṇaprabhasya //
// anena puṇyena sarveṣāṃ lokapiṭakabhājanam //
śākyabhikṣu dharmakīrttinā sattvārthe likhitaṃ śrīmad vikramaśilām āśritya
phālguṇam āse //
gnur chos kyi grags pas bris pa /
dpal ldan 'vyri krama śi lar dpye 'sla ra va la
(= gnur dharmakīrttinā śrīmadvikramaśilāyāṃ phālguṇe māse )
pratham mukhapatre (1a)---
śī la a ka ra sa bris pa (= śīlākaraṇe likhitam)
vigrahavyāvartanī pustakānte
gnur dha rma kir tis bris pa jo ca myiṅi mkhan vuyin /
etasya dharmakīrtter vaṇanaṃ debler sro po granthe /
